   controlFlag = LoginModuleControlFlag.REQUISITE;\n                break;\n            case \"SUFFICIENT\":\n                controlFlag = LoginModuleControlFlag.SUFFICIENT;\n                break;\n            case \"OPTIONAL\":\n                controlFlag = LoginModuleControlFlag.OPTIONAL;\n                break;\n            default:\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid login module control flag '\" + flag + \"' in JAAS config\");\n        }\n        return controlFlag;\n    }\n\n    private AppConfigurationEntry parseAppConfigurationEntry(StreamTokenizer tokenizer) throws IOException {\n        String loginModule = tokenizer.sval;\n        if (tokenizer.nextToken() == StreamTokenizer.TT_EOF)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Login module control flag not specified in JAAS config\");\n        LoginModuleControlFlag controlFlag = loginModuleControlFlag(tokenizer.sval);\n        Map<String, String> options = new HashMap<>();\n        while (tokenizer.nextToken() != StreamTokenizer.TT_EOF && tokenizer.ttype != ';') {\n            String key = tokenizer.sval;\n            if (tokenizer.nextToken() != '=' || tokenizer.nextToken() == StreamTokenizer.TT_EOF || tokenizer.sval == null)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Value not specified for key '\" + key + \"' in JAAS config\");\n            String value = tokenizer.sval;\n            options.put(key, value);\n        }\n        if (tokenizer.ttype != ';')\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"JAAS config entry not terminated by semi-colon\");\n        return new AppConfigurationEntry(loginModule, controlFlag, options);\n    }\n}\n","numLines":125,"startLine":1,"totalLines":125}}}

  AbstractConfig config,\n            ListenerName listenerName,\n            String clientSaslMechanism,\n            Time time,\n            LogContext logContext) {\n\n        if (securityProtocol                             AbstractConfig config,\n                                         ListenerName listenerName,\n                                         boolean isInterBrokerListener,\n                                         String clientSaslMechanism,\n                                         CredentialCache credentialCache,\n                                         DelegationTokenCache          Map<String, JaasContext> jaasContexts;\n                String sslClientAuthOverride = null;\n                if (connectionMode == ConnectionMode.SERVER) {\n                    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n                    List<String> enabledMechanisms = (List<String>) configs.get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG);\n                    jaasContexts = new HashMap<>(enabledMechanisms.size());\n                    for (String mechanism : enabledMechanisms)\n                        jaasContexts.put(mechanism, JaasContext.loadServerContext(listenerName, mechanism, configs));\n\n                    // SSL client authentication is enabled in brokers for SASL_SSL only if listener-prefixed config is specified.\n                    if (listenerName != null && securityProtocol == SecurityProtocol.SASL_SSL) {\n                        String configuredClientAuth = (String) configs.get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.SSL_CLIENT_AUTH_CONFIG);\n                        String listenerClientAuth = (String) config.originalsWithPrefix(listenerName.configPrefix(), true)\n                                .get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.SSL_CLIENT_AUTH_CONFIG);\n\n                        // If `ssl.client.auth` is configured at the listener-level, we don't set an override and SslFactory\n                        // uses the value from `configs`. If not, we propagate `sslClientAuthOverride=NONE` to SslFactory and\n                        // it applies the override to the latest configs when it is configured or reconfigured. `Note that\n                        // ssl.client.auth` cannot be dynamically altered.\n                        if (listenerClientAuth == null) {\n                            sslClientAuthOverride = SslClientAuth.NONE.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);\n                            if (configuredClientAuth != null && !configuredClientAuth.equalsIgnoreCase(SslClientAuth.NONE.name())) {\n                                log.warn(\"Broker configuration '{}' is applied only to SSL listeners. Listener-prefixed configuration can be used\" +\n                                        \" to enable SSL client authentication for SASL_SSL listeners. In future releases, broker-wide option without\" +\n                                        \" listener prefix may be applied to SASL_SSL listeners as well. All configuration options intended for specific\" +\n                                        \" listeners should be listener-prefixed.\", BrokerSecurityConfigs.SSL_CLIENT_AUTH_CONFIG);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    // Use server context for inter-broker client connections and client context for other clients\n                    JaasContext jaasContext = contextType == JaasContext.Type.CLIENT ? JaasContext.loadClientContext(configs) :\n                            JaasContext.loadServerContext(listenerName, clientSaslMechanism, configs);\n                    jaasContexts = Collections.singletonMap(clientSaslMechanism, jaasContext);\n                }\n                channelBuilder = new SaslChannelBuilder(connectionMode,\n                        jaasContexts,\n                        securityProtocol,\n                        listenerName,\n                        isInterBrokerListener,\n                        clientSaslMechanism,\n                        credentialCache,\n                        tokenCache,\n                        sslClientAuthOverride,\n                        time,\n                        logContext,\n                        apiVersionSupplier);\n                break;\n            case PLAINTEXT:\n                channelBuilder = new PlaintextChannelBuilder(listenerName);\n                break;\n            default:\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Unexpected securityProtocol \" + securityProtocol);\n        }\n\n        channelBuilder.configure(configs);\n        return channelBuilder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return a mutable RecordingMap. The elements got from RecordingMap are marked as \"used\".\n     */\n    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n    static Map<String, Object> channelBuilderConfigs(final AbstractConfig config, final ListenerName listenerName) {\n        Map<String, Object> parsedConfigs;\n        if (listenerName == null)\n            parsedConfigs = (Map<String, Object>) config.values();\n        else\n &&\n                parsedConfigs.containsKey(e.getKey().substring(listenerName.configPrefix().length()))))\n            // exclude keys like `{mechanism}.some.prop` if \"listener.name.\" prefix is present and key `some.prop` exists in parsed configs.\n            .filter(e -> !(listenerName != null && parsedConfigs.containsKey(e.getKey().substring(e.getKey().indexOf('.') + 1))))\n            .forEach(e -> parsedConfigs.put(e.getKey(), e.getValue()));\n        return parsedConfigs;\n    }\n\n    private static void requireNonNullMode(ConnectionMode connectionMode, SecurityProtocol securityProtocol) {\n        if (connectionMode == null)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"`mode` must be non-null if `securityProtocol` is `\" + securityProtocol + \"`\");\n    }\n\n    public static KafkaPrincipalBuilder createPrincipalBuilder(Map<String, ?> configs,\n                                                               KerberosShortNamer kerberosShortNamer,\n                                                               SslPrincipalMapper sslPrincipalMapper) {\n        Class<?> principalBuilderClass = (Class<?>) configs.get(BrokerSecurityConfigs.PRINCIPAL_BUILDER_CLASS_CONFIG);\n        final KafkaPrincipalBuilder builder;\n\n        if (principalBuilderClass == null || principalBuilderClass == DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder.class) {\n            builder = new DefaultKafkaPrincipalBuilder(kerberosShortNamer, sslPrincipalMapper);\n        } else if (KafkaPrincipalBuilder.class.isAssignableFrom(principalBuilderClass)) {\n            builder = (KafkaPrincipalBuilder) Utils.newInstance(principalBuilderClass);\n        } else {\n            throw new InvalidConfigurationException(\"Type \" + principalBuilderClass.getName() + \" is not \" +\n                    \"an instance of \" + KafkaPrincipalBuilder.class.getName());\n        }\n\n output.get(KRaftConfigs.NODE_ID_CONFIG)\n    if (brokerId == null && nodeId != null) {\n      output.put(ServerConfigs.BROKER_ID_CONFIG, nodeId)\n    } else if (brokerId != null && nodeId == null) {\n }\n\n  def listeners: Seq[Endpoint] =\n    CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(getString(SocketServerConfigs.LISTENERS_CONFIG), effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap)\n\n  def controllerListeners: CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(advertisedListenersProp, effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap, requireDistinctPorts=false)\n        .filter(l => controllerListenerNames.contains(l.listener))\n    } else {\n      Seq.empty\n    }\n    val controllerListenersValue = controllerListeners\n\n    controllerListenerNames.asScala.flatMap { name =>\n      controllerAdvertisedListeners\n        .find(endpoint => ListenerName.normalised(endpoint.listener).equals(ListenerName.normalised(name)))\n        .orElse(\n          // If users don't define advertised.listeners, the advertised controller listeners inherit from listeners configuration\n          // which match listener names in controller.listener.names.\n          // Removing \"0.0.0.0\" host to avoid validation errors. This is to be compatible with the old behavior before 3.9.\n          // The null or \"\" host does a reverse lookup in ListenerInfo#withWildcardHostnamesResolved.\n          controllerListenersValue\n            .find(endpoint => ListenerName.normalised(endpoint.listener).equals(ListenerName.normalised(name)))\n            .map(endpoint => if (endpoint.host == \"0.0.0.0\") {\n              new Endpoint(endpoint.listener, endpoint.securityProtocol, null, endpoint.port)\n            } else {\n              endpoint\n            })\n        )\n    }\n  }\n\n  def effectiveAdvertisedBrokerListeners: Seq[Endpoint] = {\n    // Use advertised listeners if defined, fallback to listeners otherwise\n    val advertisedListenersProp = getString(SocketServerConfigs.ADVERTISED_LISTENERS_CONFIG)\n    val advertisedListeners = if (advertisedListenersProp != null) {\n      CoreUtils.listenerListToEndPoints(advertisedListenersProp, effectiveListenerSecurityProtocolMap, requireDistinctPorts=false)\n    } else {\n      listeners\n    }\n    // Only expose broker listeners\n    advertisedListeners.filterNot(l => This callback handler is intended only to be used\n    43→ * on the Kafka broker side as it will receive a {@link OAuthBearerValidatorCallback} that includes\n    44→ * the JWT provided by the Kafka client. That JWT is validated in terms of format, expiration,\n    45→ * signature, and audience and issuer (if desired). This callback handler is the broker side of the\n    46→ * OAuth functionality, whereas {@link OAuthBearerLoginCallbackHandler} is used by clients.\n    47→ * </p>\n    48→ *\n    49→ * <p>\n    50→ * This {@link AuthenticateCallbackHandler} is enabled in the broker configuration by setting the\n    51→ * {@link org.apache.kafka.common.config.internals.BrokerSecurityConfigs#SASL_SERVER_CALLBACK_HANDLER_CLASS_CONFIG}\n    52→ * like so:\n    53→ *\n    54→ * <code>\n    55→ * listener.name.<listener name>.oauthbearer.sasl.server.callback.handler.class=org.apache.kafka.common.security.oauthbearer.OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler\n    56→ * </code>\n    57→ * </p>\n    58→ *\n    59→ * <p>\n    60→ * The JAAS configuration for OAuth is also needed. If using OAuth for inter-broker communication,\n    61→ * the options are those specified in {@link OAuthBearerLoginCallbackHandler}.\n    62→ * </p>\n    63→ *\n    64→ * <p>\n    65→ * The configuration option\n    66→ * {@link org.apache.kafka.common.config.SaslConfigs#SASL_OAUTHBEARER_JWKS_ENDPOINT_URL}\n    67→ * is also required in order to contact the OAuth/OIDC provider to retrieve the JWKS for use in\n    68→ * JWT signature validation. For example:\n    69→ *\n    70→ * <code>\n    71→ * listener.name.<listener name>.oauthbearer.sasl.oauthbearer.jwks.endpoint.url=https://example.com/oauth2/v1/keys\n    72→ * </code>\n    73→ *\n    74→ * Please see the OAuth/OIDC providers documentation for the JWKS endpoint URL.\n    75→ * </p>\n    76→ *\n    77→ * <p>\n    78→ * The following is a list of all the configuration options that jwtValidator = getConfiguredInstance(\n   108→            configs,\n   109→            saslMechanism,\n   110→            jaasConfigEntries,\n   111→            SaslConfigs.SASL_OAUTHBEARER_JWT_VALIDATOR_CLASS,\n   112→            JwtValidator.class\n   113→        );\n   114→    }\n   115→\n   116→    /*\n   117→     * Package-visible for testing.\n   118→     */\n   119→    void configure(Map<String, ?> configs,\n   120→                   String saslMechanism,\n   121→                   List<AppConfigurationEntry> jaasConfigEntries,\n   122→                   CloseableVerificationKeyResolver verificationKeyResolver,\n   123→                   JwtValidator jwtValidator) {\n   124→        this.verificationKeyResolver = verificationKeyResolver;\n   125→ Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SaslServerAuthenticator.class);\n    95→\n    96→    /**\n    97→     * The internal state transitions for initial authentication of a channel on the\n    98→     * server side are declared in order, starting with {@link #INITIAL_REQUEST} and\n    99→     * ending in either {@link #COMPLETE} or {@link #FAILED}.\n   100→     * <p>\n   101→     * Re-authentication of a channel on the server side starts with the state\n   102→     * {@link #REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE}. It may then flow to\n   103→     * {@link #REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM} before a transition to {@link #FAILED} if\n   104→     * re-authentication is attempted with a mechanism different than the original\n   105→     * one; otherwise it joins the authentication flow at the {@link #AUTHENTICATE}\n   106→     * state and likewise ends at either {@link #COMPLETE} or {@link #FAILED}.\n   107→     */\n   108→    private enum SaslState {\n   109→        INITIAL_REQUEST,               // May be SaslHandshake or ApiVersions for authentication\n   110→        HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST, // May be                    // Authentication failed\n   115→        REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE,      // Initial state for re-authentication, processes SASL handshake request\n   116→        REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM,          // When re-authentication requested with wrong mechanism, generate exception\n   117→    }\n   118→\n   119→    private final SecurityProtocol securityProtocol;\n   120→ e.getCause());\n   238→        }\n   239→    }\n   240→\n   241→    /**\n   242→     * Evaluates client responses via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse` and returns the issued challenge to the client until\n   243→     * authentication succeeds or fails.\n   244→     *\n   245→     * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\n   246→     * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\n   247→     */\n   248→    @SuppressWarnings(\"fallthrough\")\n   249→    @Override\n   250→    public void authenticate() throws IOException {\n   251→        if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\n   252→            if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\n   253→                return;\n   254→\n   255→            if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   256→                setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   257→                return;\n   258→            }\n   259→\n   260→            // allocate on heap (as opposed to any socket server memory pool)\n   261→            if (netInBuffer == null) netInBuffer = new (InvalidReceiveException e) {\n   266→                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Failing SASL authentication due to invalid receive size\", e);\n   267→            }\n   268→ the data.\n   275→        try {\n   276→            switch (saslState) {\n   277→                case REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE:\n   278→                case HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST:\n   279→                case HANDSHAKE_REQUEST:\n   280→                case INITIAL_REQUEST:\n   281→                    handleKafkaRequest(clientToken);\n   282→                    break;\n   283→ Current SASL state will be updated when outgoing writes to the client complete.\n   289→                    if (saslServer.isComplete())\n   290→                        setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   291→                    break;\n   292→                default:\n   293→                    break;\n   294→            }\n   295→        } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n   296→            // Exception will be propagated after response is sent to client\n   297→            setSaslState(SaslState.FAILED, e);\n   298→        } catch (Exception e) {\n   299→            // In the case of IOExceptions and other unexpected exceptions, fail immediately\n   300→            saslState = SaslState.FAILED;\n   301→            LOG.debug(\"Failed during {}: {}\", reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText(), e.getMessage());\n   302→            throw e;\n   303→        }\n   304→    }\n   305→\n   306→    @Override\n   307→    public KafkaPrincipal principal() {\n   308→        Optional<SSLSession> sslSession = transportLayer instanceof SslTransportLayer ?\n   309→                Optional.of(((SslTransportLayer) transportLayer).sslSession()) : Optional.empty();\n   310→        SaslAuthenticationContext context = new SaslAuthenticationContext(saslServer, securityProtocol,\n   311→                clientAddress(), listenerName.value(), sslSession);\n   312→        KafkaPrincipal principal = principalBuilder.build(context);\n   313→        if (ScramMechanism.isScram(saslMechanism) && Boolean.parseBoolean((String) saslServer.getNegotiatedProperty(ScramLoginModule.TOKEN_AUTH_CONFIG))) {\n   314→            principal.tokenAuthenticated(true);\n   315→        }\n   316→        return principal;\n   317→    }\n   318→\n   319→    @Override\n   320→    public Optional<KafkaPrincipalSerde> principalSerde() {\n   321→        return principalBuilder instanceof KafkaPrincipalSerde ? @Override\n   343→    public void reauthenticate(ReauthenticationContext reauthenticationContext) throws IOException {\n   344→        NetworkReceive saslHandshakeReceive = 419→    }\n   420→\n   421→    private void handleSaslToken(byte[] clientToken) throws IOException {\n   422→        if (!enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders) {\n   423→            byte[] response = saslServer.evaluateResponse(clientToken);\n   424→            if (saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   425→                reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n   426→ 437→            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n   438→                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n   439→            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n   440→            if (apiKey != 442→                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\n   443→                throw e;\n   444→            }\n   445→            short not supported\n   448→                // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\n   449→                throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\"Version \" + version + \" is not supported for apiKey \" + apiKey);\n   450→            }\n   451→            /*\n   452→             * The client sends multiple
